        <script>
         require(["jquery", "sv_clientLib", "lodash", "sv_goatee!plugins=cloudinary"], function($, clientLib, lodash, goatee) {
 		var node = $("#sv-smartbanner-7ba95fb2-4581-4acd-bee4-f277d1d53bdd");
 		var contentRender = node.closest(".contentRender");
 		var template = $("[data-sv-smartbanner]").html();
 		
 		var appleId = "id1015489274";
 		var googleId = "com.vamonde";
 		var $window = $(window);
 		var $body = $("body");
 		
 		var inPreview = clientLib.inPreview();
 		
 		var bannerType = clientLib.isIOS() && appleId !== "" ? "ios" :
 			clientLib.isAndroid() && googleId !== "" ? "android" :
 			inPreview && appleId !== "" ? "ios" :
 			inPreview && googleId !== "" ? "android" :
 			undefined
 		;
 		
 		// no valid banner types
 		if (bannerType === undefined) { return; }
 		
 		var storage = new clientLib.StorageCache({ type : "sessionStorage", storageKey : "plugins_core_smartbanner" });
 		// check for values which do not change over the course of a pageview, and short-circuit out
 		if (storage.get("banner-closed") === true) { return; }
 		
 		var _resizeHandler = function() {
 			// check if we are in the right conditions to load the smartbanner, if not return
 			if (inPreview && $window.width() > 1024) {
 				return;
 			}
 			
 			// valid conditions matched to show the banner, unbind the resize handler
 			$window.off("resize", resizeHandler);
 			
 			var content = goatee.fill(template, {
 				guid : "7ba95fb2-4581-4acd-bee4-f277d1d53bdd",
 				title : "Discover Chicago stories curated by experts | Powered by VAMONDE",
 				price : "FREE",
 				icon : {"raw":{"resource_type":"image","format":"jpg","pages":1,"public_id":"clients/chicago/vamonde_icon_0613fa79-d04c-4698-a30b-cf0567119e56"}},
 				id : bannerType === "ios" ? appleId : googleId,
 				bannerType : bannerType,
 				location : bannerType === "ios" ? "On the App Store" : "In Google Play",
 				url : bannerType === "ios" ? "https://itunes.apple.com/app/id1015489274" : "http://play.google.com/store/apps/details?id=com.vamonde"
 			});
 			
 			node.html(content);
 			
 			// append to the root level contentRender for the page itself, needed to get around some weird sizing sometimes applied to the first container on the page
 			contentRender.prependTo($body.find("> .contentRender"));
 			$body.addClass("smartbanner-active");
 			
 			node.on("click", ".sb-close", function(e) {
 				e.preventDefault();
 				
 				storage.set("banner-closed", true);
 				$body.removeClass("smartbanner-active smartbanner-inview");
 				node.remove();
 			});
 			
 			var nodeHeight = node.height();
 			
 			// add debounced scroll handler in order to handle switching on smartbanner-inview
 			var _scrollHandler = function() {
 				// if we are scrolled up high enough to see the smartbanner, apply the class for fixed position systems to loop into
 				$body.toggleClass("smartbanner-inview", $window.scrollTop() < nodeHeight);
 			}
 			var scrollHandler = lodash.debounce(_scrollHandler, 250, { maxWait : 250 });
 			
 			// bind the handler and call it to init the state
 			$window.on("scroll", scrollHandler);
 			scrollHandler();
 		}
 		
 		var resizeHandler = lodash.debounce(clientLib.ensureOnResize(_resizeHandler), 250);
 		
 		// bind the handler and call it to init the state
 		$window.on("resize", resizeHandler);
 		resizeHandler();
 	});
        </script>

 			{ code : "yi", label : "Yiddish" }
 		];
 
 		var html = goatee.fill(itemTemplate, { languages : languages });
 
 		root.find("[data-sv-languages]").html(html);
 
 		var readCookie = function(name) {
 			var nameEQ = name + "=";
 			var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
 			for(var i=0;i < ca.length;i++) {
 				var c = ca[i];
 				while (c.charAt(0)==' ') c = c.substring(1,c.length);
 				if (c.indexOf(nameEQ) == 0) return c.substring(nameEQ.length,c.length);
 			}
 			return null;
 		}
 
 		/* In some cases the subdomain cookie won't get deleted so google translate will retain the last
 		   translation when you navigate to a new page. This function will delete the sub-domain cookie as well. */
 		var deleteCookie = function(name) {
 			var delCookie = name + '=;expires=Thu, 01 Jan 1970 00:00:01 GMT; path=/';
 			document.cookie = delCookie;
 			document.cookie = delCookie + '; domain=.'+window.location.host;
 			document.cookie = delCookie + '; domain=.'+window.location.hostname.split('.').slice(-2).join('.');
 		}
 
 		/* Preselects the current option. In some cases the hash can disappear so we can also check for
 		   the google translate cookie if there is no hash language code */
 		var gthash = window.location.hash.match(/\#googtrans\([A-Za-z_0-9\-]+\|([A-Za-z_0-9\-]+)\)/);
 		var gtcookie = String(readCookie('googtrans')).match(/\/[A-Za-z_0-9\-]+\/([A-Za-z_0-9\-]+)/);
 		var lang =  gthash !== null ? gthash[1] : gtcookie !== null ? gtcookie[1] : "";
 		$(".googleTranslateDropdown").val(lang);
 
 		var gtTranslate = function(lang) {
 			if (lang === "") return;
 			if (lang === 'en') deleteCookie('googtrans');
 			window.location.hash = lang === 'en' ? '' : "#googtrans(en|" + lang + ")";
 			window.location.reload(true);
 		}
 
 		$('body').addClass(lang);
 
 		root.on('click', '[data-translate-select]', function() {
 			gtTranslate($(this).attr('data-value'));
 		});
 		var googleContent = $('[data-sv-googletranslate] [data-mobile-translate]');
 		$('[data-mobile-googletranslate]').append(googleContent);
 		googleContent.removeClass('hide');
 
 		$('.translateButton').on('click', function(e) {
 			e.preventDefault();
 		  $(this).next('.googleTranslateDropdown').toggleClass('dropdownOpen');
 		});
 
 	});
                    </script>
                   </div>
                  </div>
                 </div>
                </div>
               </div>
               <script>
                require(['jquery'], function($) {
 		var root = $('[data-guid="b85b2db4-b6e8-498f-b02d-9ac5860fed4d"]');
 
 		root.find('[data-translate-dropdown-trigger]').on('click', function(e) {
 			e.preventDefault();
 			root.find('[data-translate-dropdown]').toggleClass('hide');
 		});
 	});
               </script>
              </div>
             </ul>
            </div>
           </div>

             <div class="contentRender contentRender_9 contentRender_type_widget contentRender_name_plugins_search_headerbox" data-gtm-vars='{ "tCore" : { "contentNum" : "1" } }' data-sv-index="9" data-sv-time="16">
              <div class="search-wrapper show-on-large-up" data-guid-lg="b1449a59-5ce0-472b-8c2b-d50fdf4b56da" id="search_widget_headerbox_b1449a59-5ce0-472b-8c2b-d50fdf4b56da">
               <div class="search">
                <form action="/search/" class="search-form" data-sv-searchform="" method="GET">
                 <input autocapitalize="off" autocomplete="off" autocorrect="off" class="search-input" data-sv-searchinput="" name="q" placeholder="" type="search" value=""/>
                 <button class="search-icon" data-sv-searchbtn="">
                  <img src="/includes/public/assets/images/header/search_glass.gif"/>

              <div class="search-wrapper hide-for-large-up" data-guid-sm="b1449a59-5ce0-472b-8c2b-d50fdf4b56da" id="search_widget_headerbox_b1449a59-5ce0-472b-8c2b-d50fdf4b56da">
               <div class="search">
                <form action="/search/" class="search-form" data-sv-searchform="" method="GET">
                 <input autocapitalize="off" autocomplete="off" autocorrect="off" class="search-input" data-sv-searchinput="" name="q" placeholder="" type="search" value=""/>
                 <button class="search-icon" data-sv-searchbtn="">
                  <img src="/includes/public/assets/images/header/search_glass.gif"/>
                 </button>
                </form>
               </div>
              </div>
              <script>
               require(['jquery', 'plugins_search', 'jqueryui', 'domReady!'], function($, search) {
 	var sc = $('[data-sv-widgetSearchBoxContainer]').not('.insertedWidget').first();
 	var sb = $('#search_widget_headerbox_b1449a59-5ce0-472b-8c2b-d50fdf4b56da');
 	var form = sb.find('[data-sv-searchForm]');
 	var inp = form.find('[data-sv-searchInput]');
 
 	// @T300353
 	// Setup variables neeeded for autocomplete search suggestions
 	var facets = {
 		blog_leisure : "Leisure",
 		blog_blog : "Chicago Like a Local Blog",
 		blog_media : "Media",
 		blog_meetingpros : "Meeting Pros",
 		blog_travelpros : "Travel Pros",
 		blog_partners : "Partners",
 		events : "Events",
 		listings : "Listings",
 		mediagallery : "Media Gallery",
 		nav : "Pages",
 		offers : "Offers"
 	}
 	var searchLayout = new search.SearchLayout({ facets : facets });
 	var options = {
 		minLen: 2,
 		delay: 0,
 		autofill: true,
 		source: function(req, add) {
 			var searchArgs = {
 				q: req.term,
 			};
 
 			searchLayout.search(searchArgs, function(err, data) {
 				var spell = data.processed.response.spellcheck.suggestedQueries.map(function(x) {
 					return x.query;
 				});
 
 				var suggested = data.processed.response.docs.map(function(x) {
 					return x.title;
 				});
 
 				var res = spell.concat(suggested);
 
 				var unique = res.filter(function(item, pos, self) {
 					return self.indexOf(item) === pos;
 				});
 
 				add(unique);
 			});
 		},
 		open: function(event, ui) {
         	$("#ui-id-1").css("z-index", 99999);
         	$("#ui-id-1").css("display", 'block');
     	},
     	select: function(event, ui) {
     		var query = ui.item.value;
     		location.href = '/search/?q=' + query;
     	}
 	};
 
 	sc.append(sb).addClass('insertedWidget');
 	form.find('[data-sv-searchBtn]').click(function(){ form.submit(); })
 	form.submit(function(e){ if (inp.val().length === 0) { e.preventDefault(); } });
 
 	// @T300353
 	// Added autocomplete suggestions to the search box on desktop
 	inp.autocomplete(options);
 
 
 	// Mobile
 
 	var scm = $('[data-search-sm-container]');
 	var sbm = $('[data-guid-sm="b1449a59-5ce0-472b-8c2b-d50fdf4b56da"]');
 	var formm = sbm.find('[data-sv-searchForm]');
 	var inpm = formm.find('[data-sv-searchInput]');
 
 	scm.replaceWith(sbm);
 	formm.find('[data-sv-searchBtn]').click(function(){ formm.submit(); })
 	formm.submit(function(e){ if (inpm.val().length === 0) { e.preventDefault(); } });
 
 	// @T300353
 	// Added autocomplete suggestions to the search box on desktop
 	inpm.autocomplete(options);
 });
              </script>

       <script>
        require(["jquery"], function() {
 		var root = $('[data-sv-header]');
 
 		// Nav Open
 		$("[data-sv-main-nav-open]").on("click", function(){
 			var parent = $(this).parent();
 			parent.toggleClass("open");
 			$(parent.find("[data-sv-sub-nav-dropdown]")[0]).toggleClass("open");
 			$(this).find("[data-sv-toggle-icon]").toggleClass("fa-chevron-down").toggleClass("fa-chevron-up");
 		})
 
 		// Mobile Nav
 		var mobileMenu = $("[data-sv-mobile-menu]");
 		var mobileToggle = $("[data-sv-mobile-toggle]");
 		var mobileBack = $("[data-sv-mobile-back]");
 
 		mobileToggle.on('click', function(e){
 			mobileMenu.toggleClass('open');
 			mobileBack.toggleClass('open');
 		});
 
 		// This should exist in the header panel and adds the body class as quickly as possible to hide
 		// all the items on the page so we don't have the site flash before the calendar shows up
 		if (location.search.indexOf('action=popupCal') > -1 && document.body.querySelectorAll('.lookup-calHolder')) {
 			document.body.classList.add('crm-calendar-popup');
 		};
 
 
 
 		var mainNav = $("[data-sv-desktop-nav]").find('[data-sv-navigation]:first');
 		var children = mainNav.children('li.item').toArray();
 
 		function layout(item){
 			var hasBooking = Boolean($(item).find('[data-sv-has-header-booking]').length >= 1);
 			var hasImagebox = Boolean($(item).find('[data-sv-has-header-imagebox]').length >= 1);
 			var hasBothWidgets = hasImagebox && hasBooking;
 
 			if(hasBothWidgets == true){
 				$(item).find('[data-sv-columns]').addClass('small-3');
 				$(item).addClass('hasBoth');
 				$(item).find('[data-nav-widgets-container]').addClass('small-9');
 			} else if(hasBooking == true){
 				$(item).find('[data-sv-columns]').addClass('small-6');
 				$(item).find('[data-sv-columns] .nav-list').addClass('hasBooking');
 				$(item).find('[data-nav-widgets-container]').addClass('small-6');
 			} else if(hasImagebox == true){
 				$(item).find('[data-sv-columns]').addClass('small-8');
 				$(item).find('[data-sv-columns] .nav-list').addClass('hasImagebox');
 				$(item).find('[data-nav-widgets-container]').addClass('small-4');
 			} else {
 				$(item).find('[data-sv-columns]').addClass('small-12');
 				$(item).find('[data-sv-columns] .nav-list').addClass('hasNone');
 				$(item).find('[data-nav-widgets-container]').remove('[data-nav-widgets-container]');
 			}
 		}
 
 		children.forEach(layout);
 	});
       </script>

 	 		var slideCount = container.find("[data-sv-slide-count]");

 			}).on("beforeChange", function(event, slick, current, next) {

 				setSrc(root.find(".slide[data-slick-index=" + next + "] img"));

                <script>
                 require(["jquery","sv_goatee!plugins=stringLib,clientMoment,cloudinary,sv_site", "sv_clientMoment", "qs", "sv_urlLib", "sv_arrayLib", "sv_cloudinaryLib", "moment", "plugins_core", "sv_asyncLib", "sv_site", "sv_siteFoundation"], function($, goatee, clientMoment, qs, urlLib, arrayLib, sv_cloudinaryLib, moment, core, asyncLib, site, foundation) {
 
 		var root = $("[data-guid=59521f84-e9c9-45bc-aa5f-0aa92f8a5c21]");
 		var token = core.simpleToken || undefined;
 		var widgetCatData = null;
 		var eventsFormTmpl = root.find("[data-sv-eventsFormTemplate]").html();
 		var eventsListTmpl = root.find("[data-sv-eventsListTemplate]").html();
 		var widgetFeatured = "true";
 
 		var formData = {
 			startDate : clientMoment().format("l"),
 			endDate : clientMoment().add(1, "day").subtract(1, "second").format("l"),
 		}
 
 		 $(window).load(function() {
 		    renderForm();
 			search(formData);
 			continueReading();
 		}).on('resize', Foundation.utils.debounce(continueReading, 200));
 
 		root.on("click", "[data-sv-timeWindow] a", function(e) {
 			e.preventDefault();
 			setQuery($(this).attr("href"));
 			formData = qs.parse(urlLib.parse(window.location.search).query);
 			formData.startDate = $(this).attr("data-sv-startDate");
 			formData.endDate = $(this).attr("data-sv-endDate");
 			renderForm();
 			search(formData);
 		});
 
 		root.on('click', '[data-set-date]', function(e) {
 			e.preventDefault();
 			setQuery($(this).attr("href"));
 			formData = qs.parse(urlLib.parse(window.location.search).query);
 			formData.startDate = $(this).attr("data-sv-startDate");
 			formData.endDate = $(this).attr("data-sv-endDate");
 			$('[data-set-date]').not(this).parent().removeClass('active');
 			$(this).parent().addClass('active');
 			search(formData);
 		});
 
 		root.on('click', '[data-sv-continue]', function(e){
 			e.preventDefault();
 	        $(this).toggleClass("closed");
 	        root.find('[data-sv-second-row]').slideToggle();
 	        root.find('[data-sv-eventslist]').toggleClass('open');
 	        $(this).find(".fa")
 	        .toggleClass("fa-chevron-down")
 	        .toggleClass("fa-chevron-up");
 	        firstRowHeight = root.find('[data-sv-first-row]').innerHeight();
 	        root.find('[data-equalizer]').css({"min-height" : firstRowHeight + 'px'});
 	        root.foundation('equalizer', 'reflow');
 
 	    });
 
 	    function continueReading(){
 		    root.find('[data-sv-second-row]').removeClass('show');
 		    root.find("[data-sv-continue]").addClass('closed');
 		    root.find("[data-sv-continue]").find('.fa').removeClass("fa-chevron-up").addClass("fa-chevron-down");
 		}
 
 		function renderForm() {
 			var formData = qs.parse(urlLib.parse(window.location.search).query);
 			var dateFormat = dateFormat;
 
 			var date = formData.startDate || formData.endDate || clientMoment().format('M/D/YYYY');
 			var dateMoment = clientMoment(date, 'M/D/YYYY');
 			var activeDate = formData.startDate || formData.endDate || clientMoment().format('M/D/YYYY');
 			var activeDateMoment = clientMoment(activeDate, 'M/D/YYYY');
 
 			var dayData = {
 				today : clientMoment(),
 				date : dateMoment.clone(),
 				activeDate : activeDateMoment.clone(),
 				days : [],
 				arrowPageUp : dateMoment.clone().add(1, 'day'),
 				arrowPageDown : dateMoment.clone().subtract(1, 'day'),
 			};
 			var dayMoment = dateMoment.clone();
 			while(dayData.days.length < 7) {
 				dayData.days.push(dayMoment.clone());
 				dayMoment.add(1, 'day');
 			}
 
 			root.find('[data-sv-eventsFormContainer]').html(goatee.fill(eventsFormTmpl, {
 				dayData : dayData,
 				formData : formData
 			}));
 		}
 
 		function search(formData){
 			formData = qs.parse(urlLib.parse(window.location.search).query);
 			var categories_id = widgetCatData || [];
 			var filter = {}
 
 			if(widgetCatData){
 				filter.$or = widgetCatData.map(function(category) {
 					return { "categories.catId" : parseInt(category) };
 				});
 			}
 
 			if(widgetFeatured == "true"){
 				filter['featured'] = true;
 			}
 
 			if (formData.startDate == undefined){
 				formData.startDate = clientMoment().format("l")
 			}
 
 			if (formData.endDate == undefined){
 				formData.endDate = clientMoment().add(1, "day").subtract(1, "second").format("l")
 			}
 
 			filter["dates.eventDate"] = { $gte : formData.startDate, $lte : formData.endDate};
 
 			var sdate = clientMoment(moment(new Date(filter["dates.eventDate"]["$gte"] + " UTC")));
 			sdate.add(sdate.utcOffset()*-1,"m");
 			var edate = clientMoment(moment(new Date(filter["dates.eventDate"]["$lte"] + " UTC")).add(1,"d").subtract(1,"s"));
 			edate.add(edate.utcOffset()*-1,"m");
 			filter["dates.eventDate"]["$gte"] = {"$date": sdate.format()};
 			filter["dates.eventDate"]["$lte"] = {"$date": edate.format()};
 			filter["udfs_object.3601.value_string"] = "Yes"; // only include events where Show On Web is true
 
 			var options = {
 				limit: 6,
       			hooks : [
 					"afterFind_listing"
 				],
 				sort : {
 					date : 1,
 					rank : 1,
 					title : 1
 				},
 				fields : {
 					categories : 1,
 					endDate : 1,
 					location : 1,
 					media_raw : 1,
 					nextDate : 1,
 					recId : 1,
 					recid : 1,
 					startDate : 1,
 					title : 1,
 					url : 1,
 					dates : 1,
 					date : 1,
 					recurType : 1,
 					recurrence : 1,
 					featured : 1
 				}
 
 			};
 
 			$.get("/includes/rest_v2/plugins_events_events_by_date/find/", {
 				json : JSON.stringify({
 					filter : filter,
 					options : options
 				}),
 
 				token : token
 			 }).done(function(res){
 			 	data = res.docs;
 			 	data.forEach(function(item, index){
 					item["startDate"] = moment(item.start_date);
 					item["nextDate"] = moment(item.next_date);
 					item["endDate"] = moment(item.end_date);
 					item["date"] = moment(item.date);
 				});
 			 	root.find('[data-sv-eventsList]').html(goatee.fill(eventsListTmpl, {data : data}));
 			 	root.foundation('equalizer', 'reflow');
 			 });
 		}
 
 		function setQuery(href) {
 			if (href !== window.location.href) {
 				history.pushState(null, "", href);
 			}
 		}
 
 
 	});
                </script>
               </div>
              </div>
             </div>

 		var root = $("[data-guid=c809f672-d6f2-43d2-bb30-f9ccd0618309]");
 
 		
 
 		var setSrc = function(nodes) {
 			nodes.each(function(val, i) {
 				$(this).attr("src", $(this).attr("data-src"));
 				$(this).attr("onerror", $(this).attr("data-onerror"));
 			});

                 var modules = [];
 	modules.push('jquery');
 
 	
 
 	modules.push('sv_siteSlick');
 	require(modules, function($, dtn, goatee, sv_cloudinaryLib, asyncLib, objectLib) {
 		var root = $("[data-guid=10200bff-f601-4ef9-8db7-deb2a1646c54]");
 
 		
 
 		var setSrc = function(nodes) {
 			nodes.each(function(val, i) {
 				$(this).attr("src", $(this).attr("data-src"));
 				$(this).attr("onerror", $(this).attr("data-onerror"));
 			});
 		}
 
 		var slideCount = root.find("[data-sv-explore-count]");
 
 		var slider = root.find("[data-sv-explore]");
 		slider.find('.item img').removeClass('hide');
 		slider.removeClass('small-block-grid-1 large-block-grid-3');
 
 		
 			root.find('[data-sv-arrows]').removeClass('hide');
 		
 
 		slider.on("init", function(event, slick) {
 			root.css({ visibility : "visible" });
 
 			var slidesToShow = window.innerWidth > 1024 ? 3 : 1;
 			slideCount.html(Math.ceil(slick.currentSlide / slidesToShow) + 1 + "/" + Math.ceil(slick.slideCount / slidesToShow));
 		}).on("beforeChange", function(event, slick, current, next) {
 			// load the image for the next slide
 			for (var i = 0; i < slick.options.slidesToShow; i++) {
 				setSrc(root.find(".item[data-slick-index=" + (next + i) + "] img"));
 			}
 
 			var nextSlide = (next + 1) > slick.slideCount ? 1 : Math.ceil((next + 1) / slick.options.slidesToShow);
 			nextSlide = nextSlide === 0 ? 1 : nextSlide;
 			slideCount.html(nextSlide + "/" + Math.ceil(slick.slideCount / slick.options.slidesToShow));
 		});
 
 		var initializeSlick = function() {
 			slider.slick({
 				slide: '.item',
 				arrows: true,
 				prevArrow: root.find("#prevArrow"),
 				nextArrow: root.find("#nextArrow"),
 				slidesToShow: 3,
 				slidesToScroll: 3,
 				responsive: [
 					{
 						breakpoint: 1025,
 						settings: {
 							slidesToShow: 1,
 							slidesToScroll: 1
 						}
 					}
 				]
 			});
 		}
 
 		
 			initializeSlick();
 		
 	});

                <h1>
                 WELCOME To Chicago
                </h1>
                <p>
                 Welcome to Chicago, the city that feels like home. Here we have a little something for everyone. You can visit
                 <a data-sv-linklookup-id="58f6b2086d46721d2d592664" data-sv-linklookup-type="plugins_nav_navitem_primary_main" href="https://www.choosechicago.com/things-to-do/museums-and-arts/museums-galleries-and-exhibitions/" target="_self">
                  world-class museums
                 </a>
                 , dine at one of our many
                 <a data-sv-linklookup-id="58f6b21a6d46721d2d59452a" data-sv-linklookup-type="plugins_nav_navitem_primary_main" href="https://www.choosechicago.com/restaurants/foodies-and-fine-dining/michelin-guide-to-chicago/" target="_self">
                  Michelin-star restaurants
                 </a>
                 or catch a
                 <a data-sv-linklookup-id="58f6b1fc6d46721d2d59132d" data-sv-linklookup-type="plugins_nav_navitem_primary_main" href="https://www.choosechicago.com/events-and-shows/" target="_self">
                  show
                 </a>
                 in one of over 200
                 <a data-sv-linklookup-id="58f6b2086d46721d2d59269c" data-sv-linklookup-type="plugins_nav_navitem_primary_main" href="https://www.choosechicago.com/things-to-do/museums-and-arts/theater-and-performing-arts/" target="_self">
                  theaters
                 </a>
                 . No matter what you love to do, youll feel right at home doing it here.
                </p>
                <p>
                 There are plenty of
                 <a data-sv-linklookup-id="58f6b1fc6d46721d2d5912f5" data-sv-linklookup-type="plugins_nav_navitem_primary_main" href="https://www.choosechicago.com/things-to-do/" target="_self">
                  things to do in Chicago
                 </a>
                 , including
                 <a data-sv-linklookup-id="58f6b2076d46721d2d5924dc" data-sv-linklookup-type="plugins_nav_navitem_primary_main" href="https://www.choosechicago.com/things-to-do/attractions-and-tours/tours/" target="_self">
                  tours
                 </a>
                 ,
                 <a data-sv-linklookup-id="58f6b1fd6d46721d2d5915cd" data-sv-linklookup-type="plugins_nav_navitem_primary_main" href="https://www.choosechicago.com/things-to-do/chicago-sports/" target="_self">
                  spectator sports

                 ,
                 <a data-sv-linklookup-id="58f6b1fd6d46721d2d591569" data-sv-linklookup-type="plugins_nav_navitem_primary_main" href="https://www.choosechicago.com/things-to-do/shopping/" target="_self">
                  shopping

                 and other
                 <a data-sv-linklookup-id="58f6b1fc6d46721d2d591451" data-sv-linklookup-type="plugins_nav_navitem_primary_main" href="https://www.choosechicago.com/things-to-do/attractions-and-tours/" target="_self">
                  attractions

                 . Our nightlife doesn't stop either with plenty of

 				"to" : "",
 				"depart" : "",
 				"return" : "",
 				"findFlights": "",
 				"flyingFrom" : "",
 				"findPackagesIn" : "",
 				"findPackages" : "",
 				"findActivities" : "",
 				"domain" : "co.jp"
 			},
 			"de1" : {
 				"bookatrip" : "Buche eine Reise",
 				"hotels" : "Hotels",
 				"flights" : "Flge",
 				"packages" : "Angebote",
 				"activities" : "Aktivitten",
 				"findHotels" : "Finde Hotels",
 				"findHotelsIn" : "Finde Hotels in",
 				"checkIn" : "Check-in",
 				"checkOut" : "Check-out",
 				"rooms" : "Zimmer",
 				"travelers" : "Personen",
 				"from" : "Ab",
 				"to" : "Nach",
 				"depart" : "Abflug",
 				"return" : "Rckflug",
 				"findFlights": "Flug suchen",
 				"flyingFrom" : "Flge ab",
 				"findPackagesIn" : "Finde Angebote in",
 				"findPackages" : "Finde Angebote",
 				"findActivities" : "Finde Aktivitten",
 				"font" : "font",
 				"domain" : "de"
 			}
 		};
 
 		if (section === 'fr-ca') {
 			langTemplate = lang.frca;
 		} else if (section === 'pt-br') {
 			langTemplate = lang.ptbr;
 		} else if (section === 'fr1') {
 			langTemplate = lang.fr1;
 		} else if (section === 'de1') {
 			langTemplate = lang.de1;
 		} else if (section === 'es1') {
 			langTemplate = lang.es1;
 		} else if (section === 'zh1') {
 			langTemplate = lang.zh1;
 		} else if (section === 'jp') {			
 			langTemplate = lang.jp;
 		} else {
 			langTemplate = lang.default;
 		}
 
 		var html = goatee.fill(root.find('[data-booking-template]').html(), { items : langTemplate });
 		root.append(html);
 
 		// Generate Property List
 		var pipeline = [
 			{ "$match" : { "categories.catid" : 2385} },
 			{ "$match" : { "listingudfs_object.3206.value_raw" : { "$exists" : true } } },
 			{ "$project" : { "listingudfs_object.3206.value_raw" : 1 } },
 			{ "$group" : { "_id" : "$listingudfs_object.3206.value_raw" } },
 			{ "$sort" : { "_id" : 1 } },
 			{ "$project" : { "_id" : 0, "value" : "$_id" } }
 		];
 		$.get("/includes/rest_v2/plugins_listings_listings/aggregate/", {
 			json : JSON.stringify({pipeline : pipeline}),
 			token : core.simpleToken
 		}, function(data) {
 			var expediaIds = data.docs.map(function(expids) {return expids.value}).sort(function(a, b){return a-b}).join(',');
 
 			root.find('[data-sv-expIds]').val(expediaIds);
 		});
 
 		// var dateFormat = "YYYY-MM-DD";
 		var dateFormat = "MM/DD/YYYY";
 
 		var startDate = root.find('[data-sv-checkin]');
 		var endDate = root.find('[data-sv-checkout]');
 
 		
 			// Tabbed Widget
 			startDate.val(moment(new Date()).add(14, "days").format(dateFormat));
 			endDate.val(moment(new Date()).add(19, "days").format(dateFormat));
 			root.find('[data-sv-form-select]').on('click', function(e){
 				e.preventDefault();
 				root.find('[data-sv-form-select]').removeClass('active');
 				root.find('[data-sv-booking-forms]').removeClass('active');
 				$(this).addClass('active');
 				var bookingType = $(this).data('sv-form-select');
 				root.find('[data-sv-booking-forms='+bookingType+']').addClass('active');
 			})
 			startDate.datepicker({
 				onSelect : function(dateText) {
 					var thisTab = root.find('[data-sv-booking-forms].active').data('sv-booking-forms');
 					var start = moment(new Date(dateText));
 					var end = moment(endDate.datepicker("getDate"));
 					if (start.isAfter(end) || start.isSame(end)) {
 						root.find('[data-sv-booking-forms='+thisTab+'] [data-sv-checkout]').datepicker("setDate", start.add(1, 'day').toDate());
 					}
 				}
 			});
 			endDate.datepicker({
 				onSelect : function(dateText) {
 					var thisTab = root.find('[data-sv-booking-forms].active').data('sv-booking-forms');
 					var start = moment(startDate.datepicker("getDate"));
 					var end = moment(new Date(dateText));
 					if (end.isBefore(start) || end.isSame(start)) {
 						root.find('[data-sv-booking-forms='+thisTab+'] [data-sv-checkin]').datepicker("setDate", end.subtract(1, 'day').toDate());
 					}
 				}
 			});
 		
 
 		$('[data-sv-booking-forms]').submit(function(e) {
 		    e.preventDefault();
 		    var form = e.target;
 		    var values = {};
 			$.each($(form).serializeArray(), function(i, field) {
 			    values[field.name] = field.value;
 			});
 
 			var expDateFormat = "YYYY-MM-DD";
 	    	var refer = 'https://www.dpbolvw.net/click-7907203-10479934';
 	    	var InDate = moment(values.InDate).add(1,'days').format(expDateFormat);
 	    	var OutDate = moment(values.OutDate).add(1,'days').format(expDateFormat);
 
 		    if ($(form).data('form') == 'hotel') {
 		    	var urlBase = refer + '?url=https://www.expedia.' + langTemplate.domain + '/go/hotel/search/Destination/';
 		    	urlBase += InDate + '/' + OutDate;
 		    	urlBase += '?CityName=Chicago';
 		    	urlBase += '&NumRoom=' + values.NumRoom;
 		    	urlBase += '&NumAdult=' + values.NumAdult;
 		    	urlBase += '&Group=' + values.Group;
 		    	window.open(urlBase);
 		    } else if ($(form).data('form') == 'flights') {
 		    	var urlBase = refer + '?url=https://www.expedia.' + langTemplate.domain + '/go/flight/search/RoundTrip/';
 		    	urlBase += InDate + '/' + OutDate;
 		    	urlBase += '&FromAirport=' + values.FromAirport;
 		    	urlBase += '&ToAirport=' + values.ToAirport;
 		    	urlBase += '&NumAdult=' + values.NumAdult;
 		    	window.open(urlBase);
 		    } else if ($(form).data('form') == 'packages') {
 	    		var urlBase = refer + '?url=https://www.expedia.' + langTemplate.domain + '/go/package/search/FlightHotel/';
 		    	urlBase += InDate + '/' + OutDate;
 		    	urlBase += '&FromAirport=' + values.FromAirport;
 		    	urlBase += '&Destination=' + values.Destination;
 		    	urlBase += '&NumAdult=' + values.NumAdult;
 		    	window.open(urlBase);
 		     } else if ($(form).data('form') == 'activities') {
 	    		var urlBase = refer + '?url=https://www.expedia.' + langTemplate.domain + '/go/activity/search/';
 		    	urlBase += InDate + '/' + OutDate;
 		    	urlBase += '&Location=' + values.Location;
 		    	window.open(urlBase);
 		     }
 		});
 	});
                </script>
               </div>
              </div>
             </div>

              require(['jquery', 'domReady!'], function($) {
 	    var root = $('[data-guid=7c3a47c6-8fec-4b27-976e-6d0b491d205a]');
 	    var navItemProperties = JSON.parse($('meta[name=sv-nav-properties]').attr('content'));
 
 	    root.find('[data-id="' + navItemProperties.id + '"]')
 	  		.addClass('active')
 	  		.prop('selected', true);
 
 
 	  	var footerNavContent = $('[data-sv-footer-mobile-nav]').html();;
 		$('[data-sv-footer-nav-conatiner]').append(footerNavContent);
 
 		$("[data-sv-footer-nav-open]").on("click", function(){
 			var parent = $(this).parent();
 			parent.toggleClass("open");
 			$(parent.find("[data-sv-sub-nav-dropdown]")[0]).toggleClass("open");
 			$(this).find("[data-sv-toggle-icon]").toggleClass("fa-chevron-down").toggleClass("fa-chevron-up");
 		})

 		if($(".contentRender_name_plugins_core_textbox").find("img[title]").length >= 1){
